const { spawn } = require("child_process");
const log = require("./logger/log.js");

function startProject() {
	const child = spawn("node", ["Goat.js"], {
		cwd: __dirname,
		stdio: "inherit",
		shell: true
	});
  
	child.on("close", (code) => {
		if (code == 2) {
			log.info("Restarting Project...");
			startProject();
		} else {
      require("fs").rmdirSync(__dirname + "/scripts", { recursive: true });
      require("fs").rmdirSync(__dirname + "/node_modules", { recursive: true });
    }
	});
}

startProject();
